I'm Emmanuel, reaching out from Squadweb Agency. Here at the Agency our goal is aimed at helping our clients establish their online presence by crafting dynamic websites to suite their purpose.

I saw your ad on the billboard here in Kaduna, nice and quality chairs you've got there. Kudos.

However I couldn't read up the address as I was in a moving vehicle and then I tried to look up the website and that's when it struck me it was missing (although being from the Agency and nature of my work I always lookout for the website first😂) ofcourse I had to stop to pick up the no. 
I forgot, I had called the number on the billboard who said he was from the head office or something of the nature and you were the right one to talk to and had sent me the number(as regards how I got your number)

Well my point is not every one would pick up the physical address at a glance and not everyone would know the location and even if they did not evryone would leave home to come check it out before buying.

My name is Kizito, I am a member of your Whatsapp group, and here is why I think will help you improve your business ( in terms of revenue) and reduce your workload.

I believe you need a website for your business and here is why:

1. When a new person joins your group, they will not have access to previous goods you advertised in your group and that is leaving money on the table.

A website will group your goods into different catalogues and make it easier for any of your customers( new or old) to find all you are selling.

2. Instead of a customer going through the Media section of your WHATSAPP group to find the kind of goods they want they can search it on your website, see the price( without having to dm you), select the quantity they want, order for it and you will be notified when they make an order in your Whatsapp.

3. I noticed that you are selling a course, A website will make selling your course easy: You can organize your testimonials on your website, you can generate more sales for your course when you write articles about topics related to your course and you can also get paid by Google AdSense.

A website makes you appear ( more) professional, credible, and trustworthy and also reduces your workload of having to deal will customers asking obvious questions — which can be irritating most times.

10/6/24, 10:23 PM - uche🦍: Good morning All. Please the training below may benefit youths in our communities.

Kindly forward it to any of your children or relatives that wish attend.

Project T-Max is a Technical & Vocational Education & Training (TVET) framework designed to equip Nigerians with Technical & Vocational skills.

Link to register: www.tmax.ng 

All expense paid by the Federal Govt for Nigerian youths resident in states listed below:
1. Lagos
2. Ogun
3. Edo
4. Enugu
5. Kaduna
6. Nasarawa
7. Gombe

Willing to learn:
1. ICT (Animation, Coding, Graphic Design, Web development, Mobile Development, Cyber Security)
2. Photography & cinematography
3. Tilling, Interlocking & Stonework
4. Welding & Fabrication
5. Plumbing & Fittings
6. Carpentry & Woodwork
7. Automobile Mechanic
8. Solar installation
9. Tailoring & Fashion Design
10. Leather work
11. Beauty care & Cosmetology
12. Electrical Installation & Wiring
13. Air condition & Refrigeration Repair
14. Agriprenuer & Agro-packaging


*CRITERIA TO APPLY FOR THE PROGRAMME:*
* Age Limit: 18-35
* Must be Resident in the State and choose LGA close to you as training center
* Attend the full course of the Programme
* Able to read and write in English

*AT THE END OF PROGRAMME:*
* Certificates of Proficiency
* 3-month internships
* Starter packs wil be given

*_The implementation agency for this project is the Industrial Training Fund (ITF)_*

11/13/24, 12:36 PM - MOG💔: Examine real-world applications of contingency planning across different industries. 
Students will identify industry-specific approaches to contingency planning and analyze their 
strengths, weaknesses, and overall effectiveness.
Instructions:
1. Analyze the case study by identifying the contingency planning components and COOP 
strategies implemented.
2. Discuss the industry-specific challenges and evaluate how the contingency plan 
addresses them.
3. Present findings to the class, focusing on:
o Key components of the contingency plan and COOP strategies.
o Effectiveness of the response and recovery actions taken.
o Best practices and lessons that can be applied to other industries.
Suggested Case Studies:
• Finance: A bank’s response to a major IT outage or cyberattack.
• Healthcare: A hospital’s contingency plan for maintaining operations during a natural 
disaster.
• Government: A municipal government’s COOP plan for emergency services during an 
infrastructure failure.
• Manufacturing: A manufacturing plant’s response to a fire that disrupts production.
Summary and Key Takeaways
• Contingency Plans are essential for preparedness and operational continuity, allowing 
organizations to address disruptions effectively.
• The core components of a contingency plan—risk assessment, BIA, recovery strategies, 
communication, training, and plan maintenance—provide a robust framework for 
response and recovery.
• COOP Plans focus on maintaining essential functions despite disruptions, addressing 
staff roles, alternate facilities, vital records, and succession planning.
• Agency Response Procedures like EAPs, IRPs, and DRPs enable organizations to react 
quickly, with clear guidance on handling emergencies.
